                  </form>, (S, K,) or <foreign lang="ar">المَكَانَ</foreign>, (A, Mgh, Msb,) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَجُوزُ</foreign>, (S, Msb,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">جَوَازٌ</foreign> (S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">جَوْزٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جُؤُوزٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَجَازٌ</foreign>, (K,) <hi rend="ital">He went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">passed, in,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">along, the place, and left it behind;</hi> (Mgh, K;) [whether this be meant for one signification or two, does not appear; but in either case it is evident that one signification is <hi rend="ital">he passed through,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">over,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">along, and beyond, the place;</hi> and this signification is of frequent occurrence;] as also <foreign lang="ar">جاز بِهِ</foreign>; (K;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-1" target="اجازهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>; (Mgh;) and

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-3" target="تجاوزهُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6688"/></foreign>; (Mgh;) lit., <hi rend="ital">he traversed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">crossed, its</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">جَوْز</foreign>, i. e., <hi rend="ital">middle, and passed through it:</hi> (Mgh:) or <hi rend="ital">he went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">passed, in,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">along, the place;</hi> (As, S, A, Msb, TA;) as also <foreign lang="ar">جاز بِهِ</foreign>, and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-4" target="جاوزهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6685"/></foreign>, (TA,) and

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-6" target="اجتازهُ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6689"/></foreign>: (S: [so it appears from its being said that <foreign lang="ar">اِجْتِيَازٌ</foreign> is syn. with <foreign lang="ar">سُلُوكٌ</foreign>:]) and in like manner, <foreign lang="ar">الطَّرِيَقَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">the road:</hi> (TA:) <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-7" target="جاوز" n="7" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>الموضعَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">جازهُ</foreign> signify the same: (TA:) or

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-11" target="جاوزهُ" n="11" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6685"/></foreign> and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-12" target="جاوز" n="12" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بِهِ</foreign> also signify <hi rend="ital">he left it behind.</hi> (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">جُزْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">خِلَالَ الدِّيَارِ</foreign>, which is like <foreign lang="ar">جُسْتُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I passed amid,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">among, the houses:</hi> (see the remarks on the letter <foreign lang="ar">ز</foreign>:) or <hi rend="ital">I went to and fro amid,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">among, the houses,</hi> in a hostile attack upon them: or <hi rend="ital">went round about them</hi>]. (Ibn-Umm-Kásim, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">جُزْتُ بِكَذَا</foreign>, i. e., <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-13" target="اِجْتَزْتُ" n="13" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I passed by, and beyond, such a thing</hi>]. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">جاز عَلَيْهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He passed by him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">مَرَّ بِهِ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">اِمْتَرَّ بِهِ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">عَلَيْهِ</foreign>. (M and K in art. <foreign lang="ar">مر</foreign>.) And <foreign lang="ar">جَازَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He passed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">crossed, over it.</hi> (L.) <foreign lang="ar">جاز</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6684-14" target="اجاز" n="14" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6686"/></foreign> are syn. [in this last sense]. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">أَعَانَكَ ٱللّٰهُ عَلَى <ref cref="n6684-15" target="إِجَازَةِ" n="15" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>الصِّرَاطِ</foreign> (A, TA) <hi rend="ital">May God aid thee</hi> [<hi rend="ital">to pass,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">cross, over,</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">to pass along, and to leave behind thee, the Sirát.</hi> (TA.) And it is said in a trad. respecting the Sirát, <foreign lang="ar">فَأَكُونُ أَنَا وَأُمَّتِى أَوَّلَ مَنْ <ref cref="n6684-16" target="يُجِيزُ" n="16" type="6" subtype="FTFSO" lang="ar"/> عَلَيْهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And I, with my people, shall be the first who will pass over it</hi>]: <foreign lang="ar">يجيز</foreign> being here syn. with <foreign lang="ar">يَجُوزُ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">جُزْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الشَّىْءَ إِلَى غَيْرِهِ</foreign>: see 3.          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>    
      <foreign lang="ar">جاز الدِّرْهَمُ <ref cref="n6684-17" target="فَتَجَوَّزَهُ" n="17" type="1" subtype="SO" lang="ar"/></foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The piece of money passed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">was current, and he accepted it as current:</hi> in the TA written <foreign lang="ar">جاز</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الدرهم كتجوزه</foreign>, and without any syll. signs; but that the reading which I have adopted is right appears from what immediately follows:] a poet says, <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">وَزُيَّفُ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> [<hi rend="ital">Pieces of money whereof there are current and bad</hi>]: and Lh mentions the saying, <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ أَرَ النَّفَقَةَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">تَجُوزُ بِمَكَانٍ كَمَا تَجُوزُ بِمَكَّةَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I have not seen money for expenses pass away in a place as it passes away in Mekkeh</hi>]: ISd says, He has not explained it, but I think that the meaning is <foreign lang="ar">تَنْفُقُ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">جاز الشَّىْءُ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">جَوَازٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">The thing was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, allowable; it passed for lawful:</hi> as though it kept the middle (<foreign lang="ar">جَوْز</foreign>) of the road. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">جَازَ البَيْعُ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">النِّكَاحُ</foreign>, (A, Mgh,) and <foreign lang="ar">العَقْدُ وَغَيْرُهُ</foreign>, (Msb,) [<hi rend="ital">The sale,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">the marriage,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">the contract, or other thing, was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, allowable;</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">passed as right, sound, valid,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">good</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in law:</hi>] (Msb:) or <hi rend="ital">had effect.</hi> (Mgh.)                   <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">جَوْزٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">جوز</orth>
                  </form> The <hi rend="ital">middle</hi> (S, K) of a thing, (K,) or of anything; (S;) [as, for instance,] of a desert, (A,) and of a camel, (TA,) and of the night: (A, TA:) and the <hi rend="ital">main part</hi> of a thing, (K,) or of the night: (TA:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَجْوَازٌ</foreign>; (Sb, S, A;) beside which it has no other.
